        <article id="post-2444" class="et_pb_post post-2444 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-mobile-apps tag-frameworks-for-mobile-applications tag-hybrid-mobile-apps"> 
         <div class="et_post_meta_wrapper"> 
          <h1 class="entry-title">Top 5 Frameworks For Building Hybrid Mobile Applications</h1> 
          <p class="post-meta"> by <span class="author vcard"><a href="http://globussoft.com/author/jit/" title="Posts by Jit Adhikary" rel="author">Jit Adhikary</a></span> | <span class="published">Oct 3, 2016</span> | <a href="http://globussoft.com/category/products/mobile-apps/" rel="category tag">Mobile Apps</a> | <span class="comments-number"><a href="http://globussoft.com/top-5-frameworks-for-building-hybrid-mobile-applications/#respond">0 comments</a></span></p>
          <img src="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Top-5-Frameworks-For-Building-Hybrid-Mobile-Applications-1080x675.jpg" alt="Top  5 Frameworks For Building Hybrid Mobile Applications" width="1080" height="675"> 
         </div> 
         <!-- .et_post_meta_wrapper --> 
         <div class="entry-content"> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">A few years ago using JavaScript to develop mobile apps was more of a generalized attempt. However, with the passage of time, the idea of building Android and iOS apps without operating with that of Java and C (objective) started rising. &nbsp;This fact seemed to amaze most web developers. And now we have abundant frameworks to create a native mobile experience just by using web technologies.</p> 
          <h3 style="text-align: justify"><b>Introduction To <a href="https://www.quora.com/topic/Hybrid-Mobile-Applications" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff"><em>Hybrid Mobile Apps</em></span></a>:</b></h3> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">A hybridized application is more of a mobile optimized website. Mainly written in HTML, JavaScript or CSS, it consists of a well refined web-view to fit any web browser available in smartphones. The basic advantage of creating hybrid apps is to minimize the efforts of the programmer. Precisely, a program written for a particular application can be used for multiple platforms like iOS, Android and Windows phone without any modifications.</p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2446 " title="Hybrid Mobile Applications" src="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Hybrid-Mobile-Applications.jpg" alt="Hybrid Mobile Applications" width="588" height="331" srcset="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Hybrid-Mobile-Applications.jpg 1920w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Hybrid-Mobile-Applications-300x169.jpg 300w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Hybrid-Mobile-Applications-768x432.jpg 768w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Hybrid-Mobile-Applications-1024x576.jpg 1024w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Hybrid-Mobile-Applications-1080x608.jpg 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 588px) 100vw, 588px"></p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">This blog is to present a comparison between some of the popularly used JavaScript frameworks for developing hybrid applications. Most of these enlisted frameworks run unmodified application programs for <a href="http://globussoft.com/how-to-build-apps-with-cross-platform-mobile-development-tools/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff"><em>cross platforms</em></span></a>. Besides the usage of Adobe PhoneGap or Cordova along with these can facilitate the bridging of device APIs in Javascript.</p> 
          <h3 style="text-align: justify"><b>1. Ionic:</b></h3> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">Ionic is considered to be one of the most popular frameworks. Nowadays, its been the most preferred framework, being almost the primitive choice for many developers. Using Ionic can easily help in the creation of native designs just through the CSS portion of the framework. Yet a simple collaboration with AngularJS is sufficient to harness its full potential. Besides it also offers a command line interface representing some awesome features, which can be further be integrated.</p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2447 " title="Ionic framework" src="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Ionic-framework.png" alt="Ionic framework" width="588" height="301" srcset="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Ionic-framework.png 1130w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Ionic-framework-300x153.png 300w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Ionic-framework-768x393.png 768w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Ionic-framework-1024x524.png 1024w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Ionic-framework-1080x552.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 588px) 100vw, 588px"></p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><b>Advantages:</b></p> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Performs great with predefined components.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Compatible with Cordova-based application packages.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>A supreme command-line interface with useful features.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <h3 style="text-align: justify"><b>2. Framework 7:</b></h3> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">The most utilizable fact about Framework 7 is that it doesnt possess any external dependencies like Angular or React. Besides being completely framework skeptic, it manages to maintain the look and feel of native apps. To get the most out of it requires properly styled components and animations. Anyone having sufficient knowledge in CSS, HTML, and JavaScript can create apps using Framework7 without code undulation. However, it lacks tools for emulation and app packaging.</p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2448 " title="Framework 7" src="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Framework-7.png" alt="Framework 7" width="586" height="248" srcset="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Framework-7.png 1350w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Framework-7-300x127.png 300w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Framework-7-768x325.png 768w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Framework-7-1024x434.png 1024w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Framework-7-1080x458.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 586px) 100vw, 586px"></p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><b>Advantages:</b></p> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Simplified usage.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Relies mostly on JavaScript, HTML &amp; CSS.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Reliable performance.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Faster combinations with any kind of JavaScript framework.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <h3 style="text-align: justify"><b>3. Onsen UI:</b></h3> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">The Onsen UI is an open source framework that permits developers to build apps by combining native looking components. Its usage is fairly simple as it can work with or without Angular JS. Consists of a great documentation inclusive of all possible sample prototypes &nbsp;and layouts for the most common application structures.</p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2449" title="Onsen UI framework" src="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Onsen-UI-framework.png" alt="Onsen UI framework" width="589" height="290" srcset="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Onsen-UI-framework.png 1347w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Onsen-UI-framework-300x147.png 300w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Onsen-UI-framework-768x377.png 768w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Onsen-UI-framework-1024x503.png 1024w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/Onsen-UI-framework-1080x531.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 589px) 100vw, 589px"></p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><b>Advantages:</b></p> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Excellent Documentation with extensive sample prototypes.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Supports PhoneGap &amp; Cordova although builder not included.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Works effectively with predefined components.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <h3 style="text-align: justify"><b>4. JQuery mobile:</b></h3> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">jQuery being the forefather of all available mobile frameworks, hardly tries to create apps having the likes of those being used in iOS and Androids. Instead, it focuses on developing apps that work equally good on all mobile browsers. This also includes older versions like Blackberry, Symbian, Windows phone. It is light weight, depends mostly on jQuery, hence easier to learn.</p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2450 " title="JQuery mobile framework" src="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/JQuery-mobile-framework.png" alt="JQuery mobile framework" width="588" height="301" srcset="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/JQuery-mobile-framework.png 1288w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/JQuery-mobile-framework-300x153.png 300w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/JQuery-mobile-framework-768x393.png 768w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/JQuery-mobile-framework-1024x524.png 1024w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/JQuery-mobile-framework-1080x553.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 588px) 100vw, 588px"></p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><b>Advantages:</b></p> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Presents a better support for a wider range for mobile browsers.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Simplified and userfrienldy.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <h3 style="text-align: justify"><b>5. React Native:</b></h3> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">Going by its name React native serves the purpose of building proper native apps, instead of creating hybrid ones, that run in a web view. However, most of the development portion is done via JavaScript and React. This framework isnt tailored towards novice in the field of web development but certainly presents a brighter side. The presence of a huge community clarifies assistance will never be the problem. And with recent upgradations this framework even supports Android. Thus having real cross platform apps is no big deal.</p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2451 " title="React Native framework" src="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/React-Native-framework.png" alt="React Native framework" width="586" height="335" srcset="http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/React-Native-framework.png 1156w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/React-Native-framework-300x172.png 300w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/React-Native-framework-768x439.png 768w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/React-Native-framework-1024x586.png 1024w, http://globussoft.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/React-Native-framework-1080x618.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 586px) 100vw, 586px"></p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify"><b>Advantages:</b></p> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Native-like performance.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <ul style="text-align: justify"> 
           <li>Vast community.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <h3 style="text-align: justify"><b>Closure:</b></h3> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">Nothing in this world is fully compatible or entirely flawless. Similarly, every framework consists of certain cons, just like its has pros. So while making a choice be clear of its usage. In that manner, you will also be able to implement it in the right way.</p> 
          <p style="text-align: justify">Hopefully, this blog will be of great usage to you. Furthermore &nbsp;to keep an eye on more exciting and informative blogs you can <a href="http://globussoft.com/blog/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff"><em>follow</em></span></a> us. It would be considerably grateful if you share your experience with something relevant. Kindly share your opinion by leaving a comment.</p>
